[2;36m                    [0m           [1m[[0m[1;36m3[0m,[1;36m454[0m[1m][0m com.code_intelligence.jazzer.Jazzer.main [1m([0mJazzer.jav[1;92ma:77[0m[1m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A fuzzer run against an Apache POI-based extraction workflow triggered a stack      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overflow. The crash occurs deep within Java’s regular-expression engine after       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         repeated recursive calls, ultimately overflowing the thread stack. The issue is     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         reported as a `FuzzerSecurityIssue: Stack overflow`.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue:                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The trace ends in a stack overflow triggered by patterns of repeated calls to     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `java.util.regex.Pattern` matching methods [1m([0me.g., `Ques.match`, `Loop.match`,       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `GroupHead.match`, `BmpCharProperty.match`[1m)[0m interleaved thousands of times. This    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         deep recursion eventually exhausts the Java thread stack, causing the crash.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type:                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The issue is classified as a stack overflow, which can lead to denial of service  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         or untrusted code execution disruptions.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Important Observations and Findings:                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. The fuzzer harness invokes `POIXSSFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, which in turn   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         calls `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getText` on a workbook input.                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. During XML parsing [1m([0m`AbstractSAXParser`, `XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl`,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `XMLParser`, `SAXParserImpl`[1m)[0m, the `ExtendedPropertiesHandler.handleAppVersion`     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         method applies a regex via `[1;35mPattern.matcher[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.find[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Prior to regex matching, data passes through `String.getBytes` →               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `CharsetEncoder.encode` → `sun.nio.cs.CESU_8$Encoder.encodeLoop`, and through       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         tracing callbacks in `TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks`.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. The repeated regex calls suggest excessive backtracking or nested pattern      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         constructs in the expression used by `RegexRoadblocks.nodeMatchHook` [1m([0mwhich is      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         invoked via `Jazzer.guideTowardsEquality` and related instrumentation[1m)[0m.             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. The stack trace shows over [1;36m3[0m,[1;36m400[0m nested pattern-matching calls before          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         unwinding, indicating that certain crafted inputs can drive the regex engine into   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         catastrophic recursion.                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas to Investigate:                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Pattern-matching logic in `RegexRoadblocks.nodeMatchHook` and the regex passed  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to `Pattern.compile` in                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.ExtendedPropertiesHandler.handleAppVersion`.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The SAX-based event handler in `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` [1m([0mlines around     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m519[0m–[1;36m530[0m[1m)[0m that applies the regex to the “AppVersion” element.                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The interaction between the fuzzer’s data-flow tracing callbacks                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks`[1m)[0m and the built-in charset encoder                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`CESU_8$Encoder.encodeLoop`[1m)[0m.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The overall XML parsing pipeline in Apache POI that leads from                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `getExtendedProps` → `getText` → SAX parsing → handler methods.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The harness entry point [1m([0m`POIXSSFFuzzer`, `FuzzTargetRunner`, `Jazzer`[1m)[0m to      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         understand how test inputs reach the vulnerable code.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFuzzerSecurityIssue: Stack overflow[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m sun.nio.cs.CESU_8$Encoder.encodeLoop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCESU_8.jav[0m[1;92ma:542[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Identify and simplify the vulnerable regex**  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The root cause is catastrophic backtracking in  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       private static final Pattern MAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN =[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32m([0m[32m-?[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,30[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m*[0m[32m)[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.[0m[32m([0m[32m\\dc?[0m[32m)[0m[32m*[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     which uses nested quantifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` inside a `*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, leading to thousands of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecursive calls in `[0m[1;35mPattern.match[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace this with a far simpler pattern that only captures the leading “major”[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumeric portion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe only group actually used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final Pattern MAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN =[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32m([0m[32m-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,30[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This eliminates nested quantifiers altogether while still extracting the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprimary digits correctly.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Limit the size of buffered AppVersion text**  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unbounded accumulation in `appVersionBuffer` allows an attacker to send [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextremely long `<AppVersion>` content, magnifying backtracking risk and consuming [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a constant cap in the same class:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Reasonable upper bound for version strings: [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m most Excel AppVersion values are small [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m[32m"16.0"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"2010"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final int MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `[0m[1;35mhandleAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, before running the regex, check this threshold:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private void [0m[1;35mhandleAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         String appVersionString = [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.setLength[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m clear buffer promptly[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mappVersionString.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mappVersionString.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip overly long or malicious inputs[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mLOGGER.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipped AppVersion parse: length [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m exceeds [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                         [0m[1;35mappVersionString.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Matcher m = [0m[1;35mMAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN.matcher[0m[1;39m([0m[39mappVersionString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mtext.append[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"MajorVersion: "[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.append[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.append[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Optional further hardening**: in `[0m[1;35mcharacters[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, prevent [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`appVersionBuffer` from growing beyond the cap:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     @Override[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public void [0m[1;35mcharacters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m ch, int start, int length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws SAXException [0m[1;39m{[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mtext.append[0m[1;39m([0m[39mch, start, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minAppVersion[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             int remaining = MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH - [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mremaining > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 int toAppend = [0m[1;35mMath.min[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength, remaining[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.append[0m[1;39m([0m[39mch, start, toAppend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This two-pronged length check ensures that:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We never run the regex on extremely long input.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We never accumulate more than `MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH` chars.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserve existing functionality and performance**  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Most real-world AppVersion strings [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., “[0m[1;36m16.0[0m[39m”, “[0m[1;36m2013[0m[39m”, “2016c”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are under [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m characters: they remain unaffected by the [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-char cap.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The simplified regex still yields the same `[0m[1;35mgroup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for standard numeric [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The logging warning helps diagnose if legitimate Excel files ever exceed the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthreshold without causing a crash.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Justification and side-effects**  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Why optimal?** It directly addresses the backtracking hotspot by removing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnested quantifiers and stopping regex execution on unreasonably long inputs.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Logic preservation:** Normal behavior and output for valid version strings [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare unchanged; no reliance on fractional/minor version tokens was removed since [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthey were never used downstream.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Risk mitigation:** Caps and simplification prevent stack overflows and high [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCPU consumption.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Side-effects:** Very large or malformed `<AppVersion>` values will no longer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe parsed for `MajorVersion`. We log such cases for potential future adjustments [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut avoid DoS.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Testing:** Existing unit and integration tests that supply normal AppVersion[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata will continue to pass. Add a new smoke test to ensure that strings up to [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchars are still parsed.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No external, fuzzing, or harness code changes**  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All modifications reside in `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness and SAX pipeline remain untouched, preserving existing test[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand fuzz coverage without shifting the attack surface elsewhere.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
